    public abstract long getTime();

    public synchronized long getTimeMonotonic() {

        if (now > monotonic) {
            monotonic = now;
        } else {
            now = monotonic;
        }
        return now;

                return ms + msIncrease;
            }
            long nowms = org.apache.jackrabbit.oak.stats.Clock.SIMPLE.getTime();
            if (msIncrease < 10000) {
                ms += msIncrease;
                ns += msIncrease * NS_IN_MS;
                long jump = nowms - ms;
                if (jump == 0) {
                    return ms;
                } else
                    if ((0 < jump) && (jump < 100)) {
                        ns -= NS_IN_MS / 10;
                        return ms;
                    } else
                        if ((0 > jump) && (jump > (-100))) {
                            ns += NS_IN_MS / 10;
                            return ms;
                        }


            }
            if (nowms >= (ms + 1000)) {
                ms = nowms;
                ns = nowns;
            } else {
                ms = ms + 1000;
                ns = nowns + ((ms - nowms) * NS_IN_MS);
            }
            return ms;
        }

        @java.lang.Override
        public java.lang.String toString() {
            return "Clock.ACCURATE";
        }
    };

    public static class Fast extends org.apache.jackrabbit.oak.stats.Clock {
        private volatile long time = org.apache.jackrabbit.oak.stats.Clock.ACCURATE.getTime();

        public Fast(java.util.concurrent.ScheduledExecutorService executor) {
            executor.scheduleAtFixedRate(new java.lang.Runnable() {
                @java.lang.Override
                public void run() {
                    time = org.apache.jackrabbit.oak.stats.Clock.ACCURATE.getTime();
                }
            }, org.apache.jackrabbit.oak.stats.Clock.FAST_CLOCK_INTERVAL, org.apache.jackrabbit.oak.stats.Clock.FAST_CLOCK_INTERVAL, java.util.concurrent.TimeUnit.MILLISECONDS);
        }

        @java.lang.Override
        public long getTime() {
            return time;
        }

        @java.lang.Override
        public java.lang.String toString() {
            return "Clock.Fast";
        }
    }

    public static class Virtual extends org.apache.jackrabbit.oak.stats.Clock {
        private final java.util.concurrent.atomic.AtomicLong time = new java.util.concurrent.atomic.AtomicLong();

        @java.lang.Override
        public long getTime() {
            return time.getAndIncrement();
        }

        @java.lang.Override
        public void waitUntil(long timestamp) {
            long now = time.get();
            while ((now < timestamp) && (!time.compareAndSet(now, timestamp))) {
                now = time.get();
            } 
        }

        @java.lang.Override
        public java.lang.String toString() {
            return "Clock.Virtual";
        }
    }
